k_nippon = { #日本
	color = { 175 0 0 }
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	
	definite_form = yes
	
	capital = c_yamashiro
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = culture:yamato
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
}
